In[1814]:= (*RRC*)
h[t_]:=(Sinc[(Pi t)/ts] Cos[(0.5Pi t)/ts])/(1-((t)/ts)^2);
(*RRC w/timing offset*)
g[kk_,de_]:=h[ts (de+kk)];
Show[Plot[h[t],{t,-3,3},PlotStyle->Thick],Graphics[Table[Circle[{t,h[t]},{0.1,0.03}],{t,-3.001,3.001,1}]]]
Show[Plot[h[t+0.3],{t,-3,3},PlotStyle->Thick],Graphics[Table[Circle[{t,h[t+0.3]},{0.1,0.03}],{t,-3.001,3.001,1}]]]
